--S->C 公会仓库操作记录项
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO = {}
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.__index = MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.UID = 0 --物品uid
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.Apply = 0 --是否已被申请(1-被申请,0-没有)
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.ItemID = 0 --物品ID
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.StrenLvl = 0 --强化等级
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.AttrAddLvl = 0 --追加属性等级
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.GroupId = 0 --套装id
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.GroupId2 = 0 --套装id2
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.SuperNum = 0 --卓越数量
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.SuperList = nil --卓越属性列表
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.NewSuperList = nil --新卓越属性列表
MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO.m_nExistTime = 0 --存在时间

function MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.SuperList = {}
	for i=1,7 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.SuperList, MsgData_sSuperVO:New())
	end
	o.NewSuperList = {}
	for i=1,6 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.NewSuperList, MsgData_sNewSuperVO:New())
	end

	return o
end

function MsgData_sGuildWarehouseItemVO:Unpack(buffer)
	self.UID = buffer:ReadInt64()
	self.Apply = buffer:ReadInt8()
	self.ItemID = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.StrenLvl = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.AttrAddLvl = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.GroupId = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.GroupId2 = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.SuperNum = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,7 do
		self.SuperList[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
	for i=1,6 do
		self.NewSuperList[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
	self.m_nExistTime = buffer:ReadInt64()
end

--S->C 服务器通知:vip初始信息 msgId:8501
MsgData_sVipInitState = {}
MsgData_sVipInitState.__index = MsgData_sVipInitState
MsgData_sVipInitState.weekReward = 0 --周奖励未领取0领取1
MsgData_sVipInitState.weekRewardLevel = 0 --周奖励领取等级
MsgData_sVipInitState.exp = 0 --vip经验
MsgData_sVipInitState.PeriodItems = nil --剩余时间列表
MsgData_sVipInitState.LevelRewardCount = 0 --数量
MsgData_sVipInitState.LevelRewardItems = nil --vip等级奖励领取状态列表

function MsgData_sVipInitState:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.PeriodItems = {}
	for i=1,3 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.PeriodItems, MsgData_sStructPeriod:New())
	end
	o.LevelRewardItems = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sVipInitState:Unpack(buffer)
	self.weekReward = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.weekRewardLevel = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.exp = buffer:ReadInt64()
	for i=1,3 do
		self.PeriodItems[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
	self.LevelRewardCount = buffer:ReadUInt32()
	for i=1,self.LevelRewardCount do
		local tmp = MsgData_sLevelRewardState:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.LevelRewardItems, tmp)
	end
end

	end
end

MsgData_sBossChallengeRank.type = 0 --类型 0：首领挑战 1：VIP首领挑战

MsgData_sBossChallengeRank.selfDamage = 0 --个人伤害

function MsgData_sBossChallengeRank:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.list = {}
	for i=1,6 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.list, MsgData_sEliteBossRankUpdate:New())
	end

	return o
end

function MsgData_sBossChallengeRank:Unpack(buffer)
	self.type = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.selfRank = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.selfDamage = buffer:ReadInt64()
	for i=1,6 do
		self.list[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
end

--S->C 英雄洗炼信息
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem = {}
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.__index = MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.id = 0 --英雄ID
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.score = 0 --评分
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.att = 0 --攻击资质当前值
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.def = 0 --防御资质当前值
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.hp = 0 --生命资质当前值
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.cri = 0 --暴击资质当前值
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.attlimit = 0 --攻击资质上限值
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.deflimit = 0 --防御资质上限值
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.hplimit = 0 --生命资质上限值
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.crilimit = 0 --暴击资质上限值
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.attBaozi = 0 --攻击资质 0正常，1爆资
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.defBaozi = 0 --防御资质 0正常，1爆资
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.hpBaozi = 0 --生命资质 0正常，1爆资
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.criBaozi = 0 --暴击资质 0正常，1爆资
MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem.SkillList = nil --英雄技能

function MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.SkillList = {}
	for i=1,8 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.SkillList, MsgData_sHeroWashSkillItem:New())
	end

	return o
end

function MsgData_HeroWashInfoItem:Unpack(buffer)
	self.id = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.score = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.att = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.def = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.hp = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.cri = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.attlimit = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.deflimit = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.hplimit = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.crilimit = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.attBaozi = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.defBaozi = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.hpBaozi = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.criBaozi = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,8 do
		self.SkillList[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
end

MsgData_HeroInfoItem.att = 0 --攻击资质当前值
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.def = 0 --防御资质当前值
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.hp = 0 --生命资质当前值
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.cri = 0 --暴击资质当前值
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.attlimit = 0 --攻击资质上限值
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.deflimit = 0 --防御资质上限值
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.hplimit = 0 --生命资质上限值
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.crilimit = 0 --暴击资质上限值
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.attBaozi = 0 --攻击资质 0正常，1爆资
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.defBaozi = 0 --防御资质 0正常，1爆资
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.hpBaozi = 0 --生命资质 0正常，1爆资
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.criBaozi = 0 --暴击资质 0正常，1爆资
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.islock = 0 --1锁定， 0正常
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.qua = 0 --品质
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.SkillList = nil --英雄技能
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.EquipIndex = 0 --魔神装备起始位
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.Level = 0 --等级
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.Exp = 0 --当前经验
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.Grow = 0 --当前成长阶段
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.GrowExp = 0 --当前成长经验
MsgData_HeroInfoItem.JueXing = 0 --当前觉醒id

function MsgData_HeroInfoItem:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.SkillList = {}
	for i=1,8 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.SkillList, MsgData_sHeroSkillItem:New())
	end

	return o
end

function MsgData_HeroInfoItem:Unpack(buffer)
	self.id = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.chuzhan = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.star = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.power = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.score = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.skill = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.att = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.def = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.hp = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.cri = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.attlimit = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.deflimit = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.hplimit = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.crilimit = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.attBaozi = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.defBaozi = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.hpBaozi = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.criBaozi = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.islock = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.qua = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,8 do
		self.SkillList[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
	self.EquipIndex = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.Level = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.Exp = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.Grow = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.GrowExp = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.JueXing = buffer:ReadInt32()
end


--S->C 服务器通知:英雄信息(玩家登陆、更新) msgId:9985;
MsgData_sHeroInfo = {}
MsgData_sHeroInfo.__index = MsgData_sHeroInfo
MsgData_sHeroInfo.id = 0 --出战英雄ID
MsgData_sHeroInfo.fightHero = nil --所有出战英雄id，0是主出战 ，其他是副的
MsgData_sHeroInfo.count = 0 --个数
MsgData_sHeroInfo.ListVO = nil --英雄信息

function MsgData_sHeroInfo:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.fightHero = {}
	for i=1,4 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.fightHero, 0)
	end
	o.ListVO = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sHeroInfo:Unpack(buffer)
	self.id = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,4 do
		table.insert(self.fightHero, buffer:ReadInt32())
	end
	self.count = buffer:ReadUInt32()
	for i=1,self.count do
		local tmp = MsgData_HeroInfoItem:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.ListVO, tmp)
	end
end

--S->C 七日累充-信息 msgId:9989

MsgData_sSevenAccumuRT.__index = MsgData_sSevenAccumuRT
MsgData_sSevenAccumuRT.iRecharge = 0 --总充值金额
MsgData_sSevenAccumuRT.iTime = 0 --活动剩余时间
MsgData_sSevenAccumuRT.iSize = 0 --数量
MsgData_sSevenAccumuRT.ListVO = nil --已领取ID列表

function MsgData_sSevenAccumuRT:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.ListVO = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sSevenAccumuRT:Unpack(buffer)
	self.iRecharge = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iTime = buffer:ReadInt64()
	self.iSize = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,self.iSize do
		local tmp = MsgData_SevenAccumuVO:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.ListVO, tmp)
	end
end

--S->C 冲榜分页信息 msgId:7917
MsgData_sRespRushRankRT = {}
MsgData_sRespRushRankRT.__index = MsgData_sRespRushRankRT
MsgData_sRespRushRankRT.iSelfRank = 0 --自己排名，0-未上榜(上榜条件为达到最低要求)
MsgData_sRespRushRankRT.iType = 0 --冲榜类型
MsgData_sRespRushRankRT.ListVO = nil --冲榜单

function MsgData_sRespRushRankRT:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.ListVO = {}
	for i=1,50 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.ListVO, MsgData_RushRankVO:New())
	end

	return o
end

function MsgData_sRespRushRankRT:Unpack(buffer)
	self.iSelfRank = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iType = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,50 do
		self.ListVO[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
end

	self.iopen = buffer:ReadInt8()
	self.ibtn = buffer:ReadInt8()
	self.igroup = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iOpenLv = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iOpenVIP = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iOpenVIPLv = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.ipriority = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iNeedActivity = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.isort = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iAbsolutePriority = buffer:ReadInt8()
	self.szGroupName = buffer:ReadString(20)
	self.szOpenTimeAB = buffer:ReadString(20)
	self.iOpenTimeStart = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iMergeTime = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iLastTime = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iRewardTime = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iMainType = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iSubType = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.m_isRecommended = buffer:ReadInt8()
	self.m_ruleID = buffer:ReadInt16()
end

	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.ListVO = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sPartyListResult:Unpack(buffer)
	self.iSize = buffer:ReadUInt32()
	for i=1,self.iSize do
		local tmp = MsgData_PartyListVO:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.ListVO, tmp)
	end
end

	self.iIsNew = buffer:ReadInt8()
	self.iversion = buffer:ReadInt32()

		local tmp = MsgData_PartyInfoListVO:New()

		table.insert(self.ListVO, tmp)
	end
end

MsgData_sZhenfaInfo.iDan2 = 0 --资质丹数量;增加百分百
MsgData_sZhenfaInfo.iSize = 0 --阵法信息结构数量
MsgData_sZhenfaInfo.ListVO = nil --阵法信息数组

	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.ListVO = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sZhenfaInfo:Unpack(buffer)
	self.iSelectID = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iDan1 = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iDan2 = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.iSize = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,self.iSize do
		local tmp = MsgData_ZhenfaVO:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.ListVO, tmp)
	end
end

	o.ListVO = {}

	return o

	self.iSize = buffer:ReadUInt32()

		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.ListVO, tmp)
	end
end

function MsgData_sCrossPvp3PlayerMatchInfo:New()

	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.ListVO = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sCrossPvp3PlayerMatchInfo:Unpack(buffer)

	for i=1,self.iSize do
		local tmp = MsgData_CrossPvp3PlayerMatchInfoVO:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.ListVO, tmp)
	end
end

	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.ListVO = {}

	return o
end

		local tmp = MsgData_DartInfoVO:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.ListVO, tmp)
	end
end

MsgData_sGetRedPacketRank.guid = 0 --公会id
MsgData_sGetRedPacketRank.desc = "" --红包内容
MsgData_sGetRedPacketRank.count = 0 --个数
MsgData_sGetRedPacketRank.list = nil --红包领取成员list;

function MsgData_sGetRedPacketRank:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.list = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sGetRedPacketRank:Unpack(buffer)
	self.id = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.uid = buffer:ReadInt64()
	self.job = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.roleName = buffer:ReadString(32)
	self.itemId = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.getNum = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.totalNum = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.totalMoney = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.lessMoney = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.type = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.guid = buffer:ReadInt64()
	self.desc = buffer:ReadString(32)
	self.count = buffer:ReadUInt32()
	for i=1,self.count do
		local tmp = MsgData_sRedPacketMemberList:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.list, tmp)
	end
end

--S->C 寄售物品
MsgData_sConsignmentItem = {}
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.__index = MsgData_sConsignmentItem
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.uid = 0 --寄售行记录id;
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.id = 0 --物品id
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.num = 0 --数量;
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.lastTime = 0 --剩余时间
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.roleName = "" --出售者角色名字
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.price = 0 --出售单价
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.strenLvl = 0 --强化等级(翅膀时代表到期时间)
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.refinLvl = 0 --炼化等级(翅膀时代表是否特殊属性)
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.attrAddLvl = 0 --追加属性等级
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.groupId = 0 --套装id;
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.groupId2 = 0 --套装id2;
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.superNum = 0 --卓越数量
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.SupList = nil --卓越属性列表
MsgData_sConsignmentItem.NewSupList = nil --新卓越属性列表

function MsgData_sConsignmentItem:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.SupList = {}
	for i=1,7 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.SupList, MsgData_sConsignmentItemSupList:New())
	end
	o.NewSupList = {}
	for i=1,6 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.NewSupList, MsgData_sConsignmentItemNewSupList:New())
	end

	return o
end

function MsgData_sConsignmentItem:Unpack(buffer)
	self.uid = buffer:ReadInt64()
	self.id = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.num = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.lastTime = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.roleName = buffer:ReadString(32)
	self.price = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.strenLvl = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.refinLvl = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.attrAddLvl = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.groupId = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.groupId2 = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.superNum = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,7 do
		self.SupList[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
	for i=1,6 do
		self.NewSupList[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
end

MsgData_sConsignmentItemInfo.tatlPage = 0 --总页数
MsgData_sConsignmentItemInfo.count = 0 --数量
MsgData_sConsignmentItemInfo.List = nil --寄售物品列表

function MsgData_sConsignmentItemInfo:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.List = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sConsignmentItemInfo:Unpack(buffer)
	self.tp = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.curPage = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.tatlPage = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.count = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,self.count do
		local tmp = MsgData_sConsignmentItem:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.List, tmp)
	end
end

MsgData_sChainMantraInfo.list = nil --子系统开启状态

function MsgData_sChainMantraInfo:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.list = {}
	for i=1,12 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.list, MsgData_sMantraInfo:New())
	end

	return o
end

function MsgData_sChainMantraInfo:Unpack(buffer)
	for i=1,12 do
		self.list[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
end

--S->C 服务器返回:装备位信息 msgId:11032
MsgData_sEquipPosInfoNew = {}
MsgData_sEquipPosInfoNew.__index = MsgData_sEquipPosInfoNew
MsgData_sEquipPosInfoNew.selectstar = 0 --当前选中星级
MsgData_sEquipPosInfoNew.groupitems = nil --魔神套装强化信息
MsgData_sEquipPosInfoNew.count = 0 --数量
MsgData_sEquipPosInfoNew.items = nil --装备位列表

function MsgData_sEquipPosInfoNew:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.groupitems = {}
	for i=1,5 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.groupitems, MsgData_slistGodGroup:New())
	end
	o.items = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sEquipPosInfoNew:Unpack(buffer)
	self.selectstar = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,5 do
		self.groupitems[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
	self.count = buffer:ReadUInt32()
	for i=1,self.count do
		local tmp = MsgData_sEquipDataNew:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.items, tmp)
	end
end

MsgData_sEquipAddNew = {}
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.__index = MsgData_sEquipAddNew
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.uid = 0 --装备cid;
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.strenLvl = 0 --强化等级;
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.strenVal = 0 --强化值
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.attrAddLvl = 0 --追加属性等级;
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.groupId = 0 --套装id;
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.groupId2 = 0 --套装id2;
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.groupId2Bind = 0 -- 套装id2绑定状态0 未绑定，1 已绑定
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.group2Level = 0 --套装等级
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.superNum = 0 --卓越数量
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.isyuangu = 0 --是否远古
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.godLevel = 0 --神化等级
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.blessLevel = 0 --神佑等级
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.grades = 0 --品阶
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.Superitems = nil --卓越属性列表
MsgData_sEquipAddNew.NewSuperitems = nil --新卓越属性列表

function MsgData_sEquipAddNew:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.Superitems = {}
	for i=1,7 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.Superitems, MsgData_sSuperVONew:New())
	end
	o.NewSuperitems = {}
	for i=1,6 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.NewSuperitems, MsgData_sNewSuperVONew:New())
	end

	return o
end

function MsgData_sEquipAddNew:Unpack(buffer)
	self.uid = buffer:ReadInt64()
	self.strenLvl = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.strenVal = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.attrAddLvl = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.groupId = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.groupId2 = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.groupId2Bind = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.group2Level = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.superNum = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.isyuangu = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.godLevel = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.blessLevel = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.grades = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,7 do
		self.Superitems[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
	for i=1,6 do
		self.NewSuperitems[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
end

MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.StrenVal = 0 --强化值
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.RefinLevel = 0 --炼化等级
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.AttrAddLevel = 0 --追加属性等级
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.GroupId = 0 --套装id
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.GroupId2 = 0 --套装id2
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.GroupLevel = 0 --套装等级
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.SuperNum = 0 --卓越数量
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.GodLevel = 0 --神化等级
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.BlessLevel = 0 --神偌等级
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.grades = 0 --品阶
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.SuperList = nil --卓越属性列表
MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList.NewSuperList = nil --新卓越属性列表

function MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList:New()
	local o = {}
	setmetatable(o, self)

	o.SuperList = {}
	for i=1,7 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.SuperList, MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipSuperVO:New())
	end
	o.NewSuperList = {}
	for i=1,6 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.NewSuperList, MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipNewSuperVO:New())
	end

	return o
end

function MsgData_sOtherHumanItemEquipList:Unpack(buffer)
	self.TID = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.Bind = buffer:ReadInt8()
	self.StrenLevel = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.StrenVal = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.RefinLevel = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.AttrAddLevel = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.GroupId = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.GroupId2 = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.GroupLevel = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.SuperNum = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.GodLevel = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.BlessLevel = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.grades = buffer:ReadInt32()
	for i=1,7 do
		self.SuperList[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
	for i=1,6 do
		self.NewSuperList[i]:Unpack(buffer)
	end
end

	for i=1,2 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.ChapterThreat, 0)
	end
	o.ChapterFinish = {}
	for i=1,2 do  --定长数组补齐
		table.insert(o.ChapterFinish, 0)
	end
	o.Items = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sMoShenWarInfo:Unpack(buffer)
	for i=1,2 do
		table.insert(self.ChapterThreat, buffer:ReadInt32())
	end
	for i=1,2 do
		table.insert(self.ChapterFinish, buffer:ReadInt32())
	end
	self.tili = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.SecTime = buffer:ReadInt32()
	self.Count = buffer:ReadUInt32()
	for i=1,self.Count do
		local tmp = MsgData_sMoShenFubenMSWVO:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.Items, tmp)
	end
end

	o.List = {}

	return o
end

function MsgData_sDayrewardConfig:Unpack(buffer)
	self.Count = buffer:ReadUInt32()
	for i=1,self.Count do
		local tmp = MsgData_sDayrewardConfigVO:New()
		tmp:Unpack(buffer)
		table.insert(self.List, tmp)
	end
end

function MsgData_sWSDataInfo:Unpack(buffer)
	self.Count = buffer:ReadUInt32()
